And how will England and Scotland do?</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">BBC Sport&#x27;s TV and radio football pundits and co-commentators have predicted what will happen over the next five weeks, and we have asked AI and Opta&#x27;s &#x27;supercomputer&#x27; for their picks too.</p></div></div></div></div><div data-block="links" class="ssrcss-vxwoax-ComponentWrapper e1aon0op1"><div class="ssrcss-126h8e-Spacer e1aon0op0"><div spacing="4" class="ssrcss-1gccci3-Stack e1y4nx260"><ul role="list" spacing="2" class="ssrcss-94r6ik-Stack e1y4nx260"><li class="ssrcss-qzx51b-LinkItem e3eyuya1"><div spacing="4" class="ssrcss-1gccci3-Stack e1y4nx260"><a href="/sport/football/predictor/mwc2026" class="ssrcss-g7d1ie-LinkAnchor e3eyuya2"><span><p class="ssrcss-1q0s6gx-LinkHeadline e3eyuya4"><span aria-hidden="false">Play BBC Sport&#x27;s new World Cup predictor game</span></p></span><div class="ssrcss-1ulytiq-LinkIconContainer e3eyuya3"><svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" width="1em" height="1em" class="ssrcss-xi5oyi-StyledIcon e161cein1" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M21.6 14.3 5.5 31h6.4l14.6-15L11.9 1H5.5l16.1 16.7z"></path></svg></div></a></div></li></ul></div></div></div><div data-block="subheadline" class="ssrcss-vxwoax-ComponentWrapper e1aon0op1"><div class="ssrcss-usmnse-Spacer e1aon0op0"><div data-testid="subheadline"><h2 id="Who-will-win-the-World-Cup" tabindex="-1" class="ssrcss-1sc9t00-Heading e10rt3ze0"><span role="text">Who will win the World Cup?</span></h2></div></div></div><div data-block="text" class="ssrcss-vxwoax-ComponentWrapper e1aon0op1"><div class="ssrcss-126h8e-Spacer e1aon0op0"><div data-testid="rich-text"><div class="ssrcss-nqezkk-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Alan Shearer:</b> France, but there&#x27;s a caveat that comes with it - only if there is no in-house fighting. But will they meet each other in the final or before? That will be the question, but I obviously hope France will win.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Wayne Rooney: </b>England and Spain will make the final, and hopefully England will win it.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Thomas Frank: </b>France are up there of course, and Spain too because they are very clear in how they play. That gives them a massive strength, although I still doubt them a little because they rely on Lamine Yamal and Nico Williams as the wingers and, if they don&#x27;t have them, I am not sure they have enough individual quality to do it in the end.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Along with Brazil, Argentina, England and Portugal, they are the main contenders. A lot of people are saying it is France or Spain, but for me it is between Brazil and England... and I am saying England!</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Micah Richards:</b> How teams deal with the humidity is going to play a big part at this tournament, so the South American teams will be strong.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">But I just feel it&#x27;s going to be a team who are really good at keeping the ball and that points me in the direction of Spain instead. I have played there so I have been following them, and I&#x27;d like them to be the surprise of this tournament.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Sue Smith:</b> I am going for the US as the hosts who will go further than people think.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Tony Pulis: </b>Japan might have a good run at it and Norway, Morocco and Senegal are my other outsiders to watch.</p></div></div></div></div><div data-block="subheadline" class="ssrcss-vxwoax-ComponentWrapper e1aon0op1"><div class="ssrcss-usmnse-Spacer e1aon0op0"><div data-testid="subheadline"><h2 id="What-do-the-machines-think-and-do-you-agree" tabindex="-1" class="ssrcss-1sc9t00-Heading e10rt3ze0"><span role="text">What do the machines think, and do you agree?</span></h2></div></div></div><div data-block="text" class="ssrcss-vxwoax-ComponentWrapper e1aon0op1"><div class="ssrcss-126h8e-Spacer e1aon0op0"><div data-testid="rich-text"><div class="ssrcss-nqezkk-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">You&#x27;ve read what our expert humans think, but what about the machines?</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Opta&#x27;s &#x27;supercomputer&#x27; can tell you your team&#x27;s exact chances of winning any competition at any given time.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">It is actually a complex algorithm that uses a model based on betting-market odds and the sports analytics company&#x27;s own &#x27;Power Rankings&#x27;, which are calculated using past results.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">For this World Cup, it has simulated the outcome of the tournament 25,000 times - and has calculated Spain are the most likely winners (in 16.1% of the simulations).</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">France (13%), England (11.2%) and Argentina (10.4%) are also given strong chances of glory. Scotland? Not so much.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Clarke&#x27;s side are down the list in 33rd place, with only a 0.2% chance of winning the World Cup according to Opta, but on the upside, in the same simulations they got out of Group C two-thirds (66.1%) of the time.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">AI has also had its say. Its prediction was generated using Microsoft Copilot Chat - we simply asked the tool &#x27;who will win the World Cup and how will England and Scotland do?&#x27;</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Copilot Chat says Spain will win it, England will reach the semi-finals and Scotland will go out in the group stage, despite finishing third in their group.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Do you disagree with our experts? Think algorithms are for boffins, not for football?
